<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:tabletje.html>tabletje</a> (87568)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun"><a href = vnd.unilang:noun.html>Noun</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<p>Borrowed <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language"><a href = vnd.unilang:english.html>English</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">taboo</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Tongan_language" class="extiw" title="w:Tongan language">Tongan</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="to">tapu</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Polynesian" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Polynesian">Proto-Polynesian</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="poz-pol-pro">*tapu</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Oceanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Oceanic language">Proto-Oceanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="poz-oce-pro">*tabu</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Central%E2%80%93Eastern_Malayo-Polynesian_languages" class="extiw" title="w:Central–Eastern Malayo-Polynesian languages">Proto-Eastern Malayo-Polynesian</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="pqe-pro">*tambu</i>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:tachtig.html>tachtig</a> (7527)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">tachtich</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:old.html>Old</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*antahtoda</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*ahtodig</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*antahtodig</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*ahtōutēhundą</i>.

***takkewijf.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:takkewijf.html>takkewijf</a> (29604)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tak.html>tak</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:branch.html>branch</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:twig.html>twig</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-e-</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wijf.html>wijf</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:woman.html>woman</a>, bint</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun"><a href = vnd.unilang:noun.html>Noun</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:takkewijf.html>takkewijf</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:takkewijf.html>takkewijven</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">derogatory</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:a.html>A</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bitch.html>bitch</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:a.html>a</a> belligerent, annoying <a href = vnd.unilang:or.html>or</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:rude.html>rude</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:woman.html>woman</a>.</li></ol>

<p>Borrowed <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language"><a href = vnd.unilang:french.html>French</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr"><a href = vnd.unilang:talisman.html>talisman</a></i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Arabic" class="extiw" title="w:Arabic">Arabic</a></span> <i class="Arab mention" lang="ar">طِلَسْم‎</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ar-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ṭilasm</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek"><a href = vnd.unilang:ancient.html>Ancient</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:greek.html>Greek</a></a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">τέλεσμα</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">télesma</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<ul><li><b>1644</b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:johan.html>Johan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> Brune, <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:jonge.html>Jonge</a>, <i>Wetsteen <a href = vnd.unilang:der.html>der</a> vernuften</i>, publ. <a href = vnd.unilang:by.html>by</a> Iacob Lescaille, <a href = vnd.unilang:page.html>page</a> 46.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:tampon.html>tampon</a> (24032)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Nasalized <a href = vnd.unilang:variant.html>variant</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">tapon</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Frankish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Frankish language">Frankish</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*tappo</i>, <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*tappô</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:plug.html>plug</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:tap.html>tap</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, cognate <a href = vnd.unilang:with.html>with</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language"><a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tappen.html>tappe</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language"><a href = vnd.unilang:german.html>German</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Zapfen</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English"><a href = vnd.unilang:old.html>Old</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:english.html>English</a></a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">tæppa</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language"><a href = vnd.unilang:english.html>English</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:tap.html>tap</a></i>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:tandarts.html>tandarts</a> (3600)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tand.html>tand</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:tooth.html>tooth</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:arts.html>arts</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:doctor.html>doctor</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun"><a href = vnd.unilang:noun.html>Noun</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tandarts.html>tandarts</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tandartsen.html>tandartsen</a></b>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:diminutive.html>diminutive</a></i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:tandartsje.html>tandartsje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
